< Review>
I've visited this campus a couple of times while I was a student in high school. It's a relatively small college adjacent to the historic Firestone Plant and a Carl's Jr. One of the unique features that this school has is transportation. Since it's on Firestone Blvd, many students have accessibility via Metro Blue Line and the local 115 bus. Perhaps most importantly, this school has the ELAC shuttle, and it's a total advantage for students due to ridership via Monterey Park's main campus. It's free to use and I believe they operate on Mondays-Thursdays. This makes personal cars unnecessary and saves a great deal of time and money. It shouldn't be a surprise then, locals ulitlize this to their advantage and many current high school graduates, nearby, attend here. On the contrary, if I've known this if I were younger, I would've been a continuing student. However, I'm glad I didn't attend, due to many familiar faces! With that exception, it's not a horrible community college nor is it "ghetto." It's great!< /Review>

<rating>5<//rating><pics>None<//pics>< Text>
Dont judge a book by its cover!
I've lived in Beaumont for almost a year and a half and got away from my fitness regime due to there being "no desirable gyms" near by. I got to a point where I needed a Gym and was ready to get back in shape so I figured I'd check out Xtreme Fitness as it's closest to me and had the best reviews opposed to the others close by.

On the outside, the gym appears to be very small which is the main reason I never thought to sign up. Ive been in tiny gyms before and don't like that experience.

Upon taking that first step through the door and walking through the gym, I discovered its much bigger than it seems on the outside.

This gym is very well maintained and very clean, has all equipment necessary to get a great workout in no matter what your goals are, prices are very reasonable with no sign up cost and the staff is amazing. They are super nice which is very important in my book. I also appreciate their business hours, open as early as 5AM and close at 8PM (Covid hours).

Needless to say, I regret not signing up earlier and I've found my home away from home. if your hesitant about coming in and trying it,  dont be! You won't be disappointed</Text>

<Review>This is a family-owned and operated facility. Helpful and very friendly owners/staff, sufficiently spaced weights and equipment, affordable membership pricing (especially for a privately-owned gym!), plenty of beverages and snacks available for purchase to keep you hydrated and nourished during/after your workout. On-site Men's & Women's showers are a definite plus. The majority of the members I've come in contact with speak to one another, are VERY feiendly and supportive and are quick to help out and show you the correct way to use the equipment if they see you are less than knowledgeable so it's a really cool woorkout environment to be in! My two only "wish-you-could-fix" items for Xtreme are:

A) facility is not ADA accessible which prevents access to upstairs equipment and I'd really like to be able to go up there.

B) limited on-site parking leaves the adjacent gravel/dirt lot that gets FLOODED when it rains and it's difficult to step over to their paved lot and walkway so you can get to the front door. Had to give up and return home on a couple of rainy days.

However, if they do make those improvements the membership will probably no longer be affordable. Sooo... I'm content to avail myself of the equipment I AM able to access and am ao very thankful that Xtreme provides a friendly, comfortable workout experience right here in my own community!</Review><Pics>None< /Pics>< Response>

<resp>None</resp>< Review>
Cafe Rosarita is my #1 local Gringo Mexican food restaurant that has the Rosarito Mex joyous feel I only know from the late 80s into the 90s.  For me,  the Gringo surf trip people made that town fun back then.  And I feel lucky to find the Cafe Rosarito because it reminds me of them good days. The food is excellent and the atmosphere laid back, friendly and competent .  The steak special bargain is the most satisfying dish in town , or perhaps all north county SD.   Don't reveal the secret spot k38 we know.

The outside table allows your dog to be there while you eat ( note: the dog can't eat at the table - but  our dog sure loves the leftovers as soon as we're home and always complies with her best behavior )Thank you Cafe Rosarito !</Review>

I took my wife and two kids (3 y/o and 12 months) for dinner during our vacation. The service was excellent! Both waitresses that served us were kind and loved our kids. <gmapID>0x80dc71def01fd7fd:0x227b2ee53ec456db< /gmapID>< review>
The only reason I am giving this place one star is because I can't give it a zero star, which is what it deserves. My daughter and I was in Oceanside visiting with my grandson who is a Sergent in the marines and he was deploying in 2 days. My grandson suggested we try this Mexican restaurant. I was on a very small budget so I had to keep my meals to a bare bones minimum. I ordered my food, and then I asked the woman if I could get a side of sour cream. She brings me this large bowl of sour cream, which at the time I thought was very generous of her until I got my bill. The woman charged me a whopping extra $4.00 for the sour cream, which caused my bill to go up to $18.00. I didn't ask for all that sour cream, I just asked for a side of sour cream thinking it would be an extra .50 or.75.
I told her I couldn't afford an extra $4.00 on my bill because, I was on a fixed income and I had to make $60.00, which was what I had left after buying meals for the first 2 days I was there, last me another 4 days until I got home. She was very nasty, and told me she was not removing it from my bill, and that if I couldn't afford to eat out then I shouldn't have come to her restaurant.
I have dealt with a lot of nasty people in my time but to be treated with such total disregard from a restaurant owner, and the nastiness in which she spoke to me unbelievable. I will never set foot back in that place, and I suggest you check your bill thoroughly before paying it.</review>

Cafe Rosarita is pretty good /ok for a  quick (rather small) meal. They have $5.50 LUNCH "special" platter; choice of 1 of 3 ( either a beef taco or a chicken taco or a cheese enchilada, with each including beans/rice.

Overall it's ok but for the prices of most plates, it's not a lot of food, I'm thin & I never take  any back home. It's cool to try a different plate each time. < review>
Ok so I was craving Filipino food in the area and I didn't want to go to the same Filipino places that I'm used to. I wanted to try something new. So of course I pulled out my trusty yelp app and started searching and low and behold I came accross this place. It's weird how I never tried this place before because it is so close to home. Maybe because they are hidden in a small plaza. They need a bigger sign to stand out.

Ambiance is nice. Restaurant is clean. When we walked in, we were literally the second customer. Maybe because we came in on a Friday afternoon but you would think they would have more people. Anyways I didn't mind it.

We ordered the crispy pata and adobo fried rice. The crispy pata was excellent and fresh. I will definitely order it again. The adobo fried rice on the other hand was alright. It was kind of bland though.

Overall, definitely worth coming back here and trying out other items on their menu.<//review>

I also understand how a lay person wonders how someone can make an assessment so quickly.  Typically when a roof is beyond its useful life it can be determined immediately upon climbing on top of it.  There is zero benefit to our company calling a roof beyond its useful life unless it is because we do the inspections for free, don't pay our inspectors unless they sell a certification or repair, and we don't do roof replacements. < Text>
Would give this company 0 if possible. Scheduled a roof inspection. The inspector was under the impression that no one would be home, though I was home with my car parked in the garage. He sat in his car for a few minutes before pulling a ladder out of his trunk, climbing the ladder.  I could here him on the roof take a maximum of 3 steps and then turn around and get back down, fold up his ladder and place it back in the trunk. This all took place in less that 60 seconds. Now after his ‚Äúinspection‚Äù we are being told we need to replace our entire roof. I am not a roofing professional myself, but visually our roof fine, and I am very baffled how someone could inspect an entire roof and determine that it needed replacing from the top of his ladder.
